## Executive Summary
This report compares four PHASEA outputs against the same source XLSX using strict EAN normalization + checksum, title/brand checks, pack/ratio verification (dimension/capacity shielded), and adjusted-profit recomputation for multipacks. All rows printed by each report are included (no sampling). The dominant error modes are pack interpretation (multipacks and split candidates) and VERIFIED overreach when strict-exact EAN is not actually satisfied.

### Recommendations
- Best overall accuracy: **CODEX final**
- Standardize pack parsing: shield dimensions/capacity; treat 'N x capacity' as pack count N; treat '(N x M)' without units as total items N×M.
- Reserve VERIFIED strictly for checksum-valid strict exact EAN matches.
- Treat supplier-pack > amazon-pack as split/repack ambiguity: default to NEEDS VERIFICATION unless workflow explicitly supports splitting.
